Every day, there are special 'hours' in the Club lounge where you can have afternoon tea and snacks and cocktails (made to order) and canapes in the evening and it's all completely free so you can eat and drink to your heart's content. It's all delicious!Our breakfast was absolutely fantastic with a stunning view over Hong Kong as you ate. The staff in the Club area are just gorgeous. In the separate changing rooms are small steam rooms and jacuzzi's as well as showers - this area is luxurious, clean and tidy. There is also a beauty salon where I had some treatments done. THe staff are wonderful, friendly, efficient and you can't help leaving with a smile from the experience of it all.For dinner, there are several restaurants to choose from as well as bars. All were always busy and lively. Adjoining the Hotel is the Shopping Mall!! it's wonderful and plentiful and right on your doorstep!This Hotel is fantastic and we've made it a point to stay in more Langham Hotels now. Enjoy!

<Content>Great Stopover choice We stayed 3 nights on a stopover break from New Zealand. The location of the hotel is great, right next to a large shopping mall with direct access to the MTR. We would not hesitate to stay at this lovely hotel again.

<Author>RICHY-YORKS
<Content>Fantastic Christmas at the Langham Place. My wife and I spent our Christmas and New Year holiday at the Langham Place and it was the best ever. Even though it was three years since we last stayed here there was note welcoming us back. We stayed a total of nine nights and booked the Sweet Place on the 36th floor at the club level. It was well worth it for the extra room space and inclusive club benefits and facilities. Everything about the hotel was first class. The service, staff, room and food were all excellent and although some reviewers were a little unhappy about the location of the hotel we really didn鈥檛 find it an inconvenience at all. We always felt very safe when walking in the streets around the hotel and the MTR and all of the Kowloon / Hong Kong public transport links are superb. Even at it鈥檚 busiest on Christmas and New Years Eve it was really very easy to get around. Buy an Octopus card, it automatically deducts the fare as you go and can be used on just about all public transport including the Peak Tram, Star Ferry and even for small purchases in some convenience stores. It is simple to top it up and the small deposit and outstanding balance is refundable.The whole Langham Place experience from the moment we took the pre-booked hotel car on our arrival to our departure from Hong Kong airport was superb. All of the Langham Place staff at the airport and throughout the hotel were exceptional, I really can鈥檛 say enough good things about them. The hotel is great value for five star in Hong Kong and I would certainly stay here again.

<Author>MermaidPrincess77
<Content>Greatly disappointed My hubby and I first stayed at Langham Place Hotel in July 2007 for four nights. We were very happy with the Hotel's service and room that we went home and raved about it. We even recommended friends and colleagues to stay at the Hotel when they planned for trips to HK. The Hotel had created a lasting impression on us.Our next trip to HK was in Aug 2008. Naturally, we decided that we wanted to stick with Langham Place Hotel for our two nights of accommodation. We were slightly disappointed when the room that greeted us was older than the last one but everything else was fine. So, we decided that an older room would not dampen our spirits.Our last trip to HK was Dec 2008 and of course, it had to be Langham Place Hotel. Unfortunately, all the standard rooms were booked and blocked when we made our reservation nearly two months before our trip. Not ready to give up our favourite Hotel for another one, we decided to splurge on a deluxe room or what the Hotel called an Essential Place room for three nights. It would definitely be worth it, we thought. After all, we were getting a rain shower and 42 plasma flat screen TV. We even requested for a King-sized bed like we always did.However, our happy relationship with the Hotel encountered its first hiccup when the receptionist told us that our room was not ready. It was almost 3 pm. They were experiencing full house, she said, but she could give us a room with a great view...and twin beds just for that night. I was stumped and I rejected her offer. After all, I made my reservation months ahead. Full house or not, a guest expected to be given her room when it was her turn to check in.And we finally did check in after more than an hour but this time it was a Queen-sized bed instead of a King-sized bed. I requested for another change. A lady from the front desk popped by to give us our new card keys and simply walked off, leaving us to wonder what to do with the old card keys. Finally we settled down in a new room with a faulty TV remote control. We told the receptionist about it and she was supposed to send someone to fix it but nobody came.We encountered another obstacle in our relationship when we requested for two pillows from the Pillow Menu the next evening. Of course they were not available because the Hotel was having a full house. The receptionist said she would note down my request and bring me the pillows the following evening if they were available but they did not appear on our last night. Neither did anyone bother to inform us that the pillows were not coming.On the day of check-out, we waited in the queue for almost 15 minutes for our turn. Finally, a counter was free but the gentleman refused to attend to more guests. So he kept his eyes glued on his screen, occasionally looking at his colleagues on his left and right from the corner of eyes and stealing glances at the queue in front of him. He probably felt that he had attended to too many guests over the past few minutes and so, it was time for his colleagues to catch up with the number. I was fuming as we had a plane to catch. Finally, another receptionist was available and it took only a minute to complete our check-out. She did not request for our feedback on our stay, unlike previously when the Hotel was eager to find out how it fared.The relationship came to a rude end when a bell boy refused to acknowledge our presence and our huge luggage at the level one entrance. We needed to catch a cab urgently to the airport and I was trying to get the bell boy's attention but he ignored me. His attitude was shocking as we had never ever encountered a staff who was so rude during our stay at the Hotel. Where was the Hotel that we used to love? Where were the warm staff whom we thought so highly of?After a few minute, the bell boy finally asked me where we were going and I told him. No, he did not smile. In fact, none of his colleagues at the entrance were friendly. When it was our turn to board the cab, he asked me again where were were heading without making eye contact. By this time, I was simply too stunned to do anything else but repeat my destination. He remained expressionless. When we boarded the cab, the driver asked us where we were heading! Obviously, the bell boy asked us for our destination twice and still did not tell the driver where we were going! What was that about?Langham Place Hotel might have established a good reputation when it was launched, one that was good enough to help it top the TripAdvisor choice hotel chart for a long time. However, it has started to become very complacent. I was surprised when it was ousted from its top position on the chart but now I think it deserves it.

<Author>infernalman7
<Content>TripAdvisor reviews didn't let me down! What previous reviews have said were true! This hotel deserves to be on the very top list of Hong Kong. The room was very well decorated and with a little integration of technology has made it a whole lot better. The only bad thing is that internet is not free.The CISCO IP Phone thing that they have is actually quite fun to play with. Did you know that you can text (SMS) anyone in the world from that phone for free? This made my meeting with friends in Hong Kong a whole lot cheaper and easier. This was the first time that I didn't have to buy a local prepaid SIM card because of this functionality.Fitness center was very awesome. Loved the views. You should go there even if you are not planning to work out.. just for the view.As you know, it's right on top of an MTR subway station and it's only three stops away from main shopping area, Tsim Sa Tsui.Free internet at 5th Fl at Portal is quite disappointing to me. I was there during Xmas 09 and there was not enough machines! And I found out that some machines actually blocked the access to Facebook and some other websites which I don't know why. Later when I used the iMac it was fine, no blocks... strange.The shopping mall next to the hotel has the longest escalator I have ever seen in my whole life. Also, shopping there is also a great idea if you are bored at night. During Xmas, stores close even after midnight. That's what I love about Asia/Southeast Asia!Staff were very friendly. We wanted to try new places to eat but most of the places were full and had to prebook (bc it's Xmas), staff recommended a place called Goungzhou Garden in that shopping mall on the 3rd Fl. Wow the food at that place was amazing! It's Chinese food but it's also more like a fusion Chinese food more suitable for those who comes from Southeast Asia or Australia I'm sure. Should give it a try.Over all, a perfect place if you don't mind the crowd at the MTR station.

<Author>Ms.RUSK
<Content>Great location at reasonable rate for luxury hotel The Langham is a luxury hotel at a very reasonable rate. It's a very short walk to the subway that quickly and cheaply takes you anywhere you want to go in Hong Kong. There is a nice breakfast buffet every morning and a lovely pool on the roof of the building. Our room had a great view of the city, Hong Kong island, and the harbour.The only thing I didn't like about the hotel was the upsell. It was distasteful to stay at a 5-star and get an upsell for everything but the room you've already paid for. That said, we would stay here again without hesitation.

<Author>TCTroubador
<Content>High Tech High Touch Hotel This newer high rise hotel in the Mong Kok district prides itself on high tech features like a CISCO smartphone and little touches like a doorbell and tasteful lights outside your door that indicate if you don't want to be disturbed or, conversely, would like the room made up. What surprised us, though, was the fact that one entire wall of the bathroom, which ran along the tub and faced the bed, was clear glass! Is this so you can watch TV while you bathe - or is it intended for more interpersonal visions? (A shade on one side and blinds on the other allows you to make your own decisions.)Staff were uniformly helpful, often walking with us in the direction we needed to go rather than just pointing the way. Although located outside the harbor area, the hotel is connected to a large shopping center (which includes a grocery store) and a subway stop which made travel throughout the area quite easy.My only disappointment was that you have to pay extra for in-room WIFI - although there is free internet access in the Portal - Work and Play  area. If your room doesn't have a good view, be sure to take in the open pool area on the 42nd floor rooftop. Stunning.

<Author>stampwife
<Content>Lovely rooms, friendly staff My husband, daugher and I rented two Club rooms, which were great. Wonderful, comfortable beds, clean modern rooms, although not the largest we've ever stayed in. Bathroom also was new - wonderful shower with both rainbird and hand held shower fixtures, plenty of hot water, good water pressure. Also the heat/air conditioning worked well. (The three absolutes for a good hotel room - good pillow, good shower, ability to regulate the room temperature.) Paying for a room on the top floors with access to the club was more expensive but well worth it. The concierge there was very helpful. There was always something good to eat available (they have breakfast, tea, cocktails and a dessert time), it had ready computer access and was quite comfortable after walking around the packed streets of Hong Kong. You have the choice of breakfast in the club or downstairs, with the downstairs breakfast much more elaborate, with plenty of choice of food. Know, however, that everything is cleared promptly at the time they say breakfast ends. We arrived at the hotel late in the evening and left mid- morning - both times used the limo service, and again, although there was cost involved, we found it was worth the money. The location isn't the best - most americans don't stay in kowloon, we were told by local ex-pats we met, and they refer to it as the dark side,- but we found it convenient to the underground and easy to get where we wanted to go. We also wanted a more traditional experience, rather than a purely touristy one. We didn't visit the market there but did another several blocks away - mainly inexpensive but not terribly impressive goods. The attached shopping mall is exactly that - a fairly traditional shopping mall. All in all, we really enjoyed our stay.

<Author>lucywhite1980
<Content>Perfect start to a perfect honeymoon My husband and I stayed at the Langham Place for 2 nights at the start of our honeymoon. We could not have picked a better hotel!From the minute we arrived we felt so well looked after, the staff could not do enough to help us.We upgraded to a Club room which we were so pleased about-the facilities available helped make our stay so enjoyable. Drinks and snacks are available all day and they have champagne available in the evening. We chose to have breakfast in the main restaurant rather than in the Club room due to the huge choice available. There was everything you could imagine-fresh omlettes, hot Asian and Western choices, pastries, loads of fresh exotic fruit, meats, cheeses and loads more including a chocolate fountain! We especially loved the choices of fresh juice too.One of the reasons we loved the hotel so much was due to its location in what felt like 'real' HK-the streets surrounding it are really busy and lively, much different to the financial area which felt very Western. The Ladies Market is only a few streets away and is really interesting to wander round. The underground station is inside the shopping centre that the hotel is attached too which makes travelling around the city really easy.The hotels leisure facilities are also top notch, we used the gym and pool most days to relax and were not dissapointed. The rooftop pool in the evening is particularly lovely.Overall I would highly recommend this hotel to anyone no matter what your reason for being in HK.

<Content>Perfect location for 1st time visitors Going to Hong Kong for the 1st time can be a bit daunting and if you're looking for the perfect place to situate yourself, then the Langham fills the bill. Great bathroom (with a view of the city and harbour), very comfy bed with lots of soft pillows, all kinds of amenities. I can't think of anything negative about the room or the hotel. We booked breakfast in advance (130 HKD per person), great. On our last day we had to leave very early for an 8.00 AM flight to the mainland so we had breakfast in our room at 4.30 AM. At exactly 4.30 breakfast was served to our room, everything that we asked for was there.The hotel is very conveniently located in lively Mong Kok, next to the Langham Place mall and the Mong Kok MTR station. The ladies market is around the corner. The hotel is not cheap but gives excellent value for money. I can recommend this hotel to everyone with all my heart.

<Author>Sarah555
<Content>Best hotel I have ever stayed in I have to say this is the only 5 star hotel I have stayed in so I don't exactly speak from a wealth of experience, but I found the hotel to be amazingly well-equipped and well presented without being ostentatious. The staff were very attentive but not overly-so.We stayed here for our honeymoon and because the staff knew this we were given a room with a better (i.e. harbour) view and a bottle of champagne on arrival, which was a nice touch. The rooms are just amazing, and they really do give you everything you can think of, right down to the shoe-shine kit and complementary umbrella! The bed was fantastic; enormous and wonderfully comfortable. I have never slept so well.I didn't use the spa, it sounded great but was very expensive. I also didn't use the gym, though it looked to be very well-equipped and you can go on the machines while watching the sun go down across the city! The rooftop pool was very nice, and there were never more than 3 people in there when we used it. The hot tub on the roof was far too hot in my opinion! The changing rooms were excellent, with a ready supply of towels and they provide lots of useful toiletries, even deodorant, hairspray and mouthwash! They also provide combs and brushes, with a steriliser machine to keep them clean, so you really don't need to bring anything down with you when you visit. There is a sauna and steam room in both the men's and women's changing areas.One of the best things about the hotel is the amazing location. Mong Kok is the 'real' Hong Kong, with street markest, little cafes and loads and loads of shops. We were so glad we stayed here rather than on HK Island which seemed to us to be very unreal and glossy. We didn't eat in the hotel at all, as it was expensive and far too western (i.e. the signature breakfast is a Full English!). We ate Dim Sum at The London Restaurant on Nathan Road (I will do a separate review of this - head out of the hotel at street level, left on Shanghai, right on Argyle and cross over Nathan Rd and turn right, it is a couple of hundred metres along here on the left hand side). This is the most fabulous dining experience and we had brunch here every day as it was so good. There are a million diner-style eateries in the vicinity of the hotel, as there is a big eating-out culture here. They are mainly un-licensed so no beer with your noodles, you pretty much have to head to hotel restaurants if you want alcohol. You can easily get main course, rice and soft drinks for two people for around 拢7 in these street-side cafes. The Langham Place mall also has a large number of restaurants which are a little more expensive, but also a bit more civilised!As the MTR station is downstairs in the mall basement, it is very convenient when the weather is very hot, or it is chucking it down with rain, as you don't have to go outdoors to get there (however it is probably quicker if you do go out of the hotel at ground level and use the Argyle Street entrance to Mong Kok station, as gettting into the station via the mall involves a lot of standing around on very slow escalators)I could go on all day! I am SO glad we picked this hotel for our honeymoon and would thoroughly recommend it to anyone.

Also provided access to the MTR which allowed us to easily travel around (I had lived in HK 10 years ago so knew my way around).The swimming pool is on the roof and was nice and warm. The Langham Mongkok is an excellent choice.

<Author>thatsmystuff
<Content>Simply excellent They don't come much better than this. Efficient and friendly staff, stylish interior and excellent facilities - what's not to like? We stayed two nights and loved every minute of it. For a first visit to Hong Kong, it was a great choice that made us enjoy the town all the more. I would have no hesitation in booking this hotel again or in recommending it to friends.There were nice little touches from the minute we arrived at the hotel transfer desk at the airport to when we left again that put this hotel way ahead. How about an offer of something to drink and a refreshment pack when you've just come off a plane and can't wait to hit that shower? Or booking your restaurant, pre-empting all your questions about how best to get there and writing it all down for you in Chinese for the taxi before you can even begin to ask for it? Or checking your name from the room record rather than have you try to spell it out every time? In my book, it all comes down to thinking, caring staff that are doing their job properly. Full marks for that, and how I wish others would learn...Our room was on the smaller side but held our suitcases and two people without any problem, and still left us more than sufficient space to move around, work and relax. The one odd feature was the bathroom, fully exposed behind a large pane of glass. Fortunately, you could pull a shade on it. The hotel had warned that there might be trouble with the in-room WiFi system due to some works, but we experienced no problems with this. You may, instead, sometimes lose satellite TV input, but that was for brief moments and seemed to be due to weather (approaching typhoon).We only tried out the hotel's breakfast and the bar, both very good, but there are also several restaurants around if you don't feel like venturing out. There is abundant shopping and lots of restaurant options in the adjoining streets, however, and we found that the concierge makes good recommendations on these, too.

<Author>Yalee
<Content>Extremely overrated! Don't be fooled My Partner and I stayed here in late September 08. I truly can't understand the raving, salivating and gushing reviews on here.Friends of ours from Australia stayed here and also rave about it so we thought we would give it a go after we got caught up in a typhoon and could not get out of Hong Kong.We booked over wotif.com from the airport and arrived 1 hour later only to find they did't have our booking yet. The check-in girl in true Hong Kong style was rather aloof. I opened my laptop to show her the email that I recieved confirming the booking had been paid for however, this did not satisfy her. Rather than allowing me to come behind the counter and forward the email from my web mail with all the booking details and payment confirmation to the hotel, she made me wait some time for a user name and password from the internal office wif-fi system in the hotel so then I could forward the emial to their booking system. Then after she was satisfied that it was a legitimate booking, she then proceeded to fluff around for a long time before she took any details or allocated us a room. There was all manner of talking, phone calls, posing and posturing with others rather than paying attention to a customer - now correct me if I am wrong but aren't they in the hospitality business?Finally after a good 15-20 minutes we got our room. We arrived at our room and opened the door only to find we had been given a pokey substandard room that we didn't pay for with smelling carpet and a rundown cobbled together bathroom - just foul. We went back downstairs and asked for the room we actually paid for and after much fluffing around we were given a new room.  Only after some time we realised we had been given a limited mobility room........rather than moving again we decided to stay in it even though it was VERY questionable behaviour by the check-in staff to do this!We found the restaurant staff to be very rude, food way over priced and BE CAREFUL you do not order a freshly squeezed juice....this will cost 100HK or 17 AUD for a crummy glass of juice! My partner was sick and didn't order food and the waitress got irritated by it, she then proceeded to up-sell me on bread, dips, chips, drinks and anything else that could turn a $$ in lieu of my partner not ordering anything - do they have a minimum seat quota???The check-out process was another story indeed, the check-out lady seemed more interested in talking to others than helping us get checked out and to the airport to the point we had to step in and get her to focus on our check-out and stop talking to a colleague about something frivolous - something I have NEVER had to do in my life and I stay in plenty of hotels believe me!The Langham promotes itself as the most modern of hotels in Hong Kong but it doesn't even have free in-room wi-fi. All five star hotels that I have stayed in in Asia, have free in room wi-fi so I hardly think the Langham can promote itself as the latest and greatest all in all, VERY ordinary, VERY over priced and VERY misleading a 3.5 star at best!!! The bells and whistles don't account for or compensate for below average service and facilities - don't be fooled! Spend your money elsewhere for a better experience!  
<Date>Oct 3, 2008

<Content>Reserve with confidence Previous writers have rated this hotel highly and I am simply adding my fulsome praise. We stayed for a week in September 2008. <Author>mwrigh17
<Content>Great place, great hotel. We've just returned from a 6 night stay at this hotel and I can only echo all the praise extressed by fellow reviewers. Inparticular I would advise visitors to pay the extra for the club lounge - if you consider it includes breakfast which is something like 拢15 a head anyway then it's not a whole lot more. We were in and out of there all the time. It was very handy to use the lounge as a base, an extension to your room. We'd get back from visits and nip in for a drink and a nibble whatever time of day almost. It was never overly busy and we chatted to a number of people. The sinlge visitors we spoke to quite liked the fact that it was an opportunity to interact with others.The lounge is open 24 hours and acts as the reception for the club lounge rooms - I thought this was a benefit rather than an issue as has been stated by another reviewer. Be aware though that despite what the same reviewer said alcoholic drinks disappear at 01:00 until 06:00 - apart from bottled beer and soft drinks. Sometimes they did run out of sparkling wine and champagne too. Cocktails are DIY and there is no whisky - only about 6 bottles of branded spirits - gin, vodka, baileys, etcFood in the loung is nibbles - hot and cold - and there are set times for breakfast, lunch, afternoon tea and supper. They take the food away after these times and are pretty smart about doing so. We found it perfectly adequate so didn't require to eat out hardly at all and people often took soft drinks away with them for their day out. The gym is very well stocked and never gets busy. The changing area has a sauna and steam room and has all the disposable products you require and more besides - I hardly opened my own wash bag whilst I was there!It's a great hotel but what sets it apart is the lounge - it took a lot of the stress out of the break for us.

<Author>WeekendBreaks
<Content>Great location Myself and my husband stayed here at the end of our honeymoon. We stayed in 3 hotels in Thailand before we arrived in Hong Kong. We had arranged the hotels car pick up service which was fast  efficient. On arrival at the hotel we were being led to the main check-in desk however as we were staying in a club room we shoudve been taken straight up to the lounge to check in. I had emailed the hotel letting them know we were on honeymoon and they said they would have champagne for us but we didnt get any. We were disappointed after the fantastic treatment we received in the hotels in Thailand.The room was on the 38th floor and we had an amazing view and could even see the harbour. We went to the club lounge every evening. We found the drinks selection limited with only one type of red or white wine and on 2 occassions there wasnt any wine left. Champagne was nice though! Sometimes it was hard to relax in the lounge as there was a lot of business deals going on around us. The internet access was handy too except when you had to wait ages to get on a computer.The suite was big and had a kitchen. we didnt use it but look out for the free haagen daz hiding in the freezer!! The bed was so comfy with lots of pillows.The location is excellent and with the fantastic subway system you can get around very easily and cheaply. The markets near the hotel are excellent. We had to buy an extra suitcase (in the market of course) to take all our purchases home. The hotel provide a free guided tour of the markets and shopping near the hotel - this is a great way of getting to know your way around the area. We had breakfast in the hotel and it was plentiful with a great choice. We had the buffet one evening but found it quite expensive. We also used the chuan spa and got massages which were ideal before our long flights home. If you are going to Hong Kong then definately stay here. You are only a few stops away from the harbour area and will get a better experience staying in Mong kok.

<Author>atcer28
<Content>Excellent value and great service at the Langham Place I have just returned from a 3 night stay in a club room at the Langham Place and would definately recommend this hotel to anyone, particularly the club rooms. Check in is done in the club lounge which was the only problem I had with this hotel. There was always a wait at the club desk whenever I went there including check in and check out as they seem to be doing the job of concierge and front desk for all the club rooms. At least you can enjoy a drink in comfort whilst you wait! The staff were always very friendly and efficient and apologetic if you had to wait.The room itself was on the small side but average for Hong Kong. However it had every amenity I could want with a modern bathroom with huge bath tub which you could watch TV in and separate rainshower. It had a huge LCD TV screen, DVD player and ipod dock. There was fresh fruit in the room and 2 bottles of free mineral water every day as well. The views were very good over to Hong kong island from the 35th floor.The club lounge was the best bit about this room. There was a selection of 7 different wines on offer 24 hours plus all the usual other drinks, all self service. There was also breakfast, afternoon tea, Mumm champagne, cocktails and a wide selection of canapes and a pudding buffet at various times. You could quite easily not need to eat much else during the day apart from the club food! There were 4 computer terminals, massage chairs and a selection of reading material too. I deceided to have breakfast in the main restaurant as it had a wider selection with everything from sushi and dim sum to omelettes and baked beans.I enjoyed the hotel pool which is outdoors on the roof. It is very modern and sleek by design with day beds and very comfortable loungers and free ipod rental as well. I used the spa and that was excellent - one of the best I have used. I recommend the heavenly scalp and foot treatment after a long flight. I also received a discount for this by booking in advance through the hotel website.Location wise Mongkok seemed perfectly safe to a single female wondering around. It is only a few blocks from Ladies market and the MTR is in the adjoining shopping mall. The mall itself had a large selection of restaurants, cafes, shops and a supermarket.I would definately stay at in this hotel again when I return to Hong Kong

<Content>Totally Excellent Experience! Having just got married in Fiji we arrived in Hong Kong for the start of our honeymoon. I had chosen the Langham Place Hotel from the reviews on Trip Advisor. I booked my accommodation direct with the hotel and was very impressed with the efficiency they showed with my booking\enquiries. Everything from the efficiency of the booking process to the warm welcome we received from the 'Pink Ladies' made our stay in Hong Kong extremely pleasant.Having worked in 5 star hotels myself, i can honestly say this hotel definately lives up to its 5 star status. We had a room on the 26th floor which has the most wonderful view looking back into the main city of Hong Kong. Located in Mong Kok the hotel is close to the ladies market as well as the best place to buy electronics. Pay no attention to any feedback about Mong Kok not being a nice looking place. Remember that you are not in 'Kansas' anymore as i felt like i was experiencing the 'true' Hong Kong. The hotel is excellently located to the MRT which we used everyday. The MRT is even better than the cheap taxis that are prevalent around Hong Kong as it is fast and cheap (although quite crowded at times but thats the wonder of Hong Kong!). Food outside of the hotel was cheap and abundant. Walking around we felt completely safe although you do tend to feel a bit worried when the stall owners chase you down the street when you dont buy thier goods (if they are really keen on selling you something they will keep offering you a lower price and hound you until you cave in but its all done in a very friendly manner).Price wise this hotel is very resonable. The money we saved on accommodation we spend at the stores! Due to our wonderful experience both my new wife and i will be returning to Hong Kong and we will definately be staying at the Langham Place Hotel again!

<Author>sandinmyshoe
<Content>disapointing second visit This is my second stay at the Langham Place, my last visit was two years ago. The hotel has a good location in Mongkok, which is a slightly run down area but is safe for tourists, with easy access to a number of attractions and shopping areas, the primary reason for most peoples visit. The MTR is next to the hotel, although taxis are cheap and more convienient. The hotel has a good sized gym with a roof top pool, and the well equipped changing rooms feature a sauna, steam room and hot tub. Although showing signs of wear, the rooms are fairly spacious with nice bathrooms. Service at the restaurants and reception was efficient , but fairly clinical, I unsuccesfully attempted to arrange a late check out from my room , a simple and reasonable request, but I was advised to contact my travel agent in the UK as this would be easier ! If this is your first visit to HK you won't be disappointed with this hotels location and facilities, however for returning visitors or the more discerning traveller there are better alternatives available.

<Author>KingDoody
<Content>Best Hotel we have stayed in! We stayed at the Langham Place for 5 nights in August and were not disappointed. My wife and I both agreed that is probably the best hotel we have ever stayed in.Hotel staff could not be more helpful and the standards of cleanliness in the rooms and elsewhere was excellent.Rooms are not huge but of a very high standard.Food quality is also superb and multi-cultural.The only slight negative point was the hotel's location, in that it is in a working class area of Kowloon that is not the most pleasant area to walk around (especially late at night). All TV channels not working properly - had to get housekeeping to send their technician to reprogram the TV5. Mildew in the shower 6. Haven't heard from anyone from the Langham!ConclusionFrom what we have read on tripadvisor, we either weren't staying at the Langham Mongkok or must be the unluckiest people on earth to find such a room in the Langham Mongkok. I sometimes wonder where we would have ended up without the upgrade - windowless room in the basement??? It is a real pity that we had all these problems with the room as most of the staff were beyond reproach and it is clear that the hotel does have most of the ingredients to be outstanding. It seems that I wasn't able to check another email they sent correcting their earlier email saying that it was all arranged. So I had to waste my precious vacation time emailing the travel agency  fretting over this. The next morning, the travel agency emailed me that they already extended my stay. I forwarded this email to the reservations group with a message that I hope everything is all cleared. It wasn't. After a whole day of shopping, tired and sore, the keys to the room weren't working! Had to go down to the front desk . They informed me that I was supposed to be checked out already! It seems that the reservations group was still waiting for further email confirmation from the travel agency. Couldn't they have just taken my forwarded email at face value? Or couldn't they just have called the agency? I spoke with the duty manager and said that I wasn't okay anymore. She sent me a new key right away and said they were sorry for the situation. I sent Langham an email regarding my experience but still no response 1 day later.

<Author>swastikrath
<Content>Nice Stay at the Langham Place We chose the Langham Place after reading the reviews on Tripadvisor...and we were not disappointed. We spent 2 nights at the Langham Place last weekend.We took the Airport Shuttle and reached the Hotel at around 12 Noon. I had booked an experience package and we were given a room immediately on arrival, even though check-in time was 3 PM.We were offered cold towels, and were presented with Welcome Drink vouchers and a complimentary Mongkok Guide book. (Much helpful), and were given a room on the 26th floor. Room was small but well equipped, view from the room was nothing to write home about. We did try the room service that night and the food was excellent, compliments to the chef... However we preferred to walk across the lobby and into the Langham Place Mall food court for the remaining days. I would recommend the food court. The food is cheaper and they have quite a large variety on offer.The Bar was quite a decent place to lounge around in, DJ early in the evening and then a live band later in the evening.Computers with high speed internet connections were available complimentary for guests near the Lounge. I used them to check in online for my return flight. I would however have loved it if they had provided free internet access in the rooms.We had booked the Hong Kong Island tour through the Hotel and the tour organized was excellent. Available: Large Plasma TV, DVD Player (However no DVDs), Cisco IP Phone, useful to check your account, however didn't find any use for it other than that. What sets the Hotel apart is the staff. They go out of the way to be of service. They even allowed me a late checkout , no questions asked. I would just stay here for the service. However I would expect more value for money.

<Author>AJZ
<Content>Will be back! We chose this hotel based on the reviews on TP and also personal recommendation by friend of a friend. We stayed 5 nights in Aug. We had a 3-bed room (king size and a single bed) and although small for European and definitely American standards, it was adequate and normal for HK standards. We had a room on the 27th floor and the views are amazing. IT facilities in the room are really good and loved the IP phone, IPOD docking facilities. Cupboard storage space was small for 3 people; enough for the few days but not for 2 weeks. Positives on the hotel:1. Fantastic views.2. Excellent, friendly and helpful staff from the cleaner, doorman, concierge, check in staff. 3. Location for us was excellent. It is connected to a shopping centre and Mong Kok MTR is right under the shopping centre. This is my 7th visit to HK and I find the location works really well for us. It is not in traditional tourist land of Tsim Sha Tsui, Wan Chai, Central or Causeway bay. As a result, you get a better feel of real HK. There are not any of the guys trying to sell you tourist stuff. Prices are also cheaper here. A camera we bought was 800 HK dollar cheaper in Mong Kok than in Harbour City. 4. Swimming pool and sun bathing area is really good. On the 42nd floor, the views are amazing.5. Free computer use on the rest area is really good. However, trying to get on to them was sometimes difficult. There is a policy of 20 mins but some guests seem to ignore this.6. We booked directly on hotel website. When we arrived, we were not aware that the prices had lowered compared to the time we booked. The hotel gave us the lowered advertised price which I thought was very nice. Definite plus for customer loyalty! Only one negative:1. Breakfast might have been good. We took the no breakfast option which we would recommend. The day we decided to try out the breakfast, it was 10.20 and breakfast stopped at 10.30. They showed us our table, but by the time we got to pick our breakfast, the food was getting packed away. So we rushed around trying to pick up what was not being very quickly packed away. Why let us have a table if the food was going to be put away so quickly. Felt very cheated on paying nearly 200 HK dollar each for some cereal, tea and bread. There are plenty eateries for breakfast. We ate at Delifrance and McDonalds. There is a Starbucks in the shopping centre. All in all, excellent stay and will be back soon!

<Author>DanielDP
<Content>Cannot go wrong with it, what everyone says is true: GREAT HOTEL I chose this hotel a/because of the excellent reviews, b/because of the convenient location in Kowloon. I wasn't disappointed. Although the rooms are the usual HK size, they are impeccably clean, have ALL you need and more, and the service is attentive and professional. I would go for a higher-floor executive room next time, although my standard one was cozy and modernly furnished. You have to pay for internet, which is probably something I would have expected included in the price, and with WI-FI and not just cable..The breakfast a-la-carte is good, and there are many closeby restaurants both in Mongkok and in the attached shopping mall that you can reach the Lobby floor.The laundry service is expensive and the ironing is not great, but if you need your clothes done fast, you cannot choose a better place. I found the overall quality to be very high and the price reasonable for Hong Kong. I strongly recommend it unless you can of course stay in one of the 5star hotels near the bay..

<Content>Above average We stayed here at the end of our 17 day trip to China and we were a little tired of traveling by the time we hit Hong Kong. I did not find this hotel as compelling as other reviewers. I am not that picky and there is nothing really to complain about with the exception of the pretty small rooms. I was a little disappointed. I would advise checking out the other top class hotels in the city as well.

<Content>Loved the Langham The Langham Place in Hong Kong is an awesome hotel. All I really need to say to sum it up is that you can order different flavored pillows. There is even a pillow menu that describes each flavor and its benefits. This is the level of service at the Langham. If you decide to stay, you should stay on the floors where you get access to the club room. This room features free drinks and internet along with a place to lounge and relax in your very own massage chair. The hotel鈥檚 rooms are very spacious for the city and feature excellent views. They are very pleasantly decorated and the beds are good. The cleanliness of the bathroom is reassured as it features glass walls, which do take a little getting used to. The location is convenient to get to the MTR. In fact, you don鈥檛 even have to go outside to get to the station. The hotel is also attached to an insanely large mall and is near Ladies Market.

<Author>AustRob
<Content>My #1 Hotel Stay ever Absolutely fantastic, best hotel experience i have had.Me and my girlfriend decided to have a 2 day stop over in hong kong on our way back to Australia from the UK. The room could not be faulted whatsoever, the standard was fantastic and beautiful.Views were phenomenal, with views of the light show at night and the hong kong cityscape.Service was fantastic, unfortunately my girlfriend had an accident were DARK PURPLE nail polish was spilt on the carpet, now at most other western hotels im sure we would of been looked down on us for the rest of the trip and ultimately charged for cleaning etc. Not here, they just sent up the correct people, cleaned it, the service standard did not change and we were not charged for the steam cleaning.Food was also absolutely fantastic, we ate in on the first night and got room service and the quality of the food was very good. One of the best meals i have had in a long time.The location is ideal, being a short walk to the MTR, Buses, Ladies Market, Computer Market and much more. I dont think you could get anywhere more ideally placed if you tried.The value for money was impeccable, being about the same price for an 'acceptable hotel' in Australia or the UK. I would gladly come back to this hotel if i was in Hong Kong.

<Author>mikelynn
<Content>What a "Place" Have just moved on from a 4 night stay at Langham Place, luckily moved just before the storm hit Hong Kong. Stayed in room on 31st floor, an executive room. Excellent view of Kowloon and could just about see the harbour from the big windows. Rooms are compact but big enough unless you are stuck in it all day. Amenities are good, bathroom nice, tv large with some english language channels, iphone thing useful if you have an ipod to plug in it. Breakfast was really good, lots of choices from dim sum to Japanese, smoked salmon, full cooked english (british) and healthy options also. The staff throughout are very friendly and helpful be that at breakfast or on the front desk. The bar areas are ok in a hotel sort of way, quite stylish but a bit soul less, a dj does play some tunes a couple of night a week but nothing too heavy. The pool area is tiny and ok for a swim if you wanted to cool down after a day in the humidity.The location of the hotel is close to an MTR so handy for connections and backs onto a shopping mall. Mongkok is a real Chinese enclave not touristy at all and all more an experience for that. We would stay here again if we came back.

Access to the members lounge well worth it, had a few drinks there every night and some food after tours and shopping. Breakfast is better in the main area but much busier than the lounge. Loved the luxury but being left alone at the same time. Buy an Oyster card, well worth it. Not really worth getting the train up the Peak as you can't see anything. You can use your Oyster card on the star ferry and then get a bus to the Peak - better than making your way into town, walking and joining the long queue for this short journey. If you are vegetarian remember that most of the food contains oyster sauce ! for fast food, recommend curry in a hurry within the mall.

<Author>KarlManila
<Content>Diamond in the Rough Diamond in the Rough.My girlfriend and I stayed at LHP for 2 nights. It's in Mongkok, and all of the happening places are about 15-20 minutes away by train, and 100 HKD by taxi. It would really be helpful if you buy the 3-day MTR pass if staying at LHP. Now the good part...We stayed at the Club Rooms, and it was pretty standard because it wasn't that spacious. The exclusivity was key because not anyone may access rooms above the 36th floor. It was always well maintained and all the amenities were first class.It was definitely a room for honeymooners or a weekend getaway with a loved one. Then theres CLub L. Its a quaint lobby on the 36th floor that serves as a chill out lounge with all your hedonistic needs. They offer snacks and drinks 24-7, breakfast until 11am, cocktails and champagne from 6-8pm, and massage chairs that face a huge fish tank, etc, etc, etc. all these for FREE. I was blown away with the amenities because you can basically just pig out in the lounge area, eat some good cheese, drink champagne, and enjoy the view, and not worry about paying for anything. It feels like you're at home, and yet have first class service. On our last day, since our flight was at 9:55pm, they let us stay and lounge and settle down before the long trip home. I figured, after a long and tiring day of shopping around the city, if we had no place to rest, relax and recharge, our trip would have ended awful. Fortunately, Langham Place gave the best service and provided the best amenities. Full props to its professional and very accomodating staff! My girlfriend and I can't stop talking about it on our way back home. Nice.

<Author>TravelingJournal
<Content>The people make the difference If you expect people in HK to speak English fluently, I think you would be disappointed that most people do not speak the language, or at least pretend that they do not know. If not for the hotel staff in providing me with the utmost detail of what I needed to know, I would have had difficulty navigating through the streets of HK. I was especially thankful of Stephen Poon, the assistant manager on duty the evening of my arrival. Without his willingness to help my wife and I, our honeymoon through HK would not have been as good. The staff at the Langham will take the extra effort to make your time worthwhile. The facility itself is clean and neatly organized. The rooms might not be big, but they are made for the techie that I am. If you have not checked out the bathrooms, check out other people's photos. Yes they are transparent.The hotel sits in a pretty interesting area of the city. If you walk out to the Eastern exit, you will encounter the various shopping districts of Hong Kong from the ladies market to the electronics mecca of HK. To the Western side you can find the local street market where they sell anything from live chicken and seafood to the strangest looking so called food you can ever find anywhere. In all, a good place to stay. BTW, we ordered the pickup and dropoff service to the airport provided by the hotel (at a cost of course), and was happy with the service even if it was not cheap. It was convenient to have someone take you from door to door without much hassle.

<Author>Brian&Alan
<Content>Good Value for Money The Langham Place is on Kowloon and in a great location. However, don't be fooled into thinking you will get any harbour view from here. You won't. We stayed in a Club room ( on the same floor as the Club Lounge ) It was a nice room, with a great bathroom. The room size is a little compact but it was all we needed for a two night stay. We used the lounge facilities every morning for breakfast, and again for cocktails in the evening. The IT facilities in the lounge are also first class and available 24hrs. We ate at the restaturant one lunch time which was actually quite good considering it was a buffet. The hotel is connected to a good mall so there is plenty of choice close by. We took a cab to the Star ferry to cross over to Hong Kong island. Cabs are relatively cheap here. The pool on the top floor has a great aspect over the city skyline and was quite a cool place to hang out for a couple of hours one evening. We took the bus service from the airport which was great as The Langham Place is the first stop in Kowloon. We ordered the limo service for the return journey which was seamless and a nice treat. Overall, the hotel is really good. Great value for money considering how expensive Hong Kong hotels are. The rooms are a little on the small side, and we didnt get to check into our room until 1pm (despite arriving at 0800) However, the Hotel did allow us use the lounge facilities until our room become available which was well appreciated. Will definetly stay here again. Highly recommended.

<Author>VentureTraveler
<Content>Loved the Langham We read many reviews, and tried to find a hotel in Hong Kong that offered luxury, but at a relatively affordable price. We wound up booking the Langham in Mong Kok. We booked a 2 room suite on the club floor through the hotel's web site (which I would highly recommend surfing, it's a little complex but the best deals for this hotel are there), at a little over $400 per night. While, as most people state, we found it a little out of the way, the hotel was wonderful. First, I would highly recommend the club floor rooms. the rooms are higher up, offering relief from the claustrophobia of Hong Kong. Second, the club lounge was excellent - and, like the rest of the hotel, it just grows and grows on you. It's open 24 hours, unheard of in this day and age, and offers breakfast, many courses of light appetizers, sweets at night, and drinks of all kinds, both soft and alcoholic, and champagne at certain hours. It also has 2 massage chairs, a business center with MAC's and PC's and printers, a DVD lending library, nice seating, and a nice staff, and expresso maker (which I loved, expresso every day, and excellent expresso at that). Next, the rooms. while they were a bit smallish for a suite, they had wonderful fit-and-finish, comfortable beds, 2 bathrooms and 2 flat panel TV's. Add a nice pillow menu (try it, they're not kidding, order your own pillow and it will be cheerfully delivered), internet phones with color displays, free internet access. All in, you're quite comfortable. Oh, I might add, and this was not clear at all (either from reading TripAdvisor or from the staff), if you're staying on the club floor, you can go down to the lobby restaurant for the sumptuous full breakfast (it's downright decadent), for FREE! It's probably the largest breakfast buffet I've ever seen (and I travel extensively). The only way we figured this out was to take a table and try it, as we got conflicting answers from the staff as to whether it was included in the club floor rate or not.The hotel also has an excellent Gym, nice locker rooms, slippers, fluffy robes, turndown service, an assortment of magazines in your room when you get there, daily newspapers, and more. The spa area was particularly nice and you don't need to go to a spa treatment to use it. The rooftop pool was also great, and if you want to venture further in the hotel, there is a complete business center on the 5th or 6th floor with about a dozen computers. Use of the computers is free. The one thing I would point out is that this hotel IS out of the way. On Sunday morning (no pedestrian traffic), it took us about 30 minutes at a steady, brisk walk to get to the Kowloon waterfront. I highly recommend taking cabs (and I usually walk everywhere), they are excellent, incredibly cheap, and very helpful. I think our average cab ride was about $4 anywhere in Kowloon. I can't wait to go again.

<Author>tmelon
<Content>Great hotel. Awesome location. We just stayed at Langham Place in Hong Kong for 5 nites in May. It was a great location. Connected to a large shopping mall and a MTR station. To go to the MTR station, you can walk indoor all the way. The shopping mall has a supermarket. It was easy to get snacks and drinks. The food court in the shopping mall was great also. There are many great shopping places around the hotel. Within walking distance. In regards to the hotel, we love the room. It is a bit small for the price. For less $, you can get a suite (with a living room) at Eaton Hotel which is close by. But the rest of the room is great. Very clean. We do not understand how everything can sparkle after each cleaning. The shower was sooooo clean. The maid also goes out of her way to give us bottles of water when she sees us come back from a long day of shopping! However, it was a bit disappointing that the room smells musky if the A/C is off for a short time. Try to keep it on. We also had trouble with getting both English and Chinese newspaper. They do not understand that we would like both; tried to explain 3 days in a row (and I speak Cantonese). My husband does not read Chinese even though he looks Chinese. In summary, we loved it despite these little things. We will consider going back there but will probably pay more for a bigger room.

<Author>verymodest
<Content>One of Our Favorite Hotels in Asia We just finished our stay at Langham Place Hotel. This one is an absolute gem. We loved our stay here. First of all, this is a classy hotel with amazing service and outstanding amenities. The rooms are excellent and include very confortable beds, a large-screen plasma TV, internet and spectacular views. There is excellent food in the restaurants. The breakfast is very luxurious. The Temple Street Night Market is just a short 15 minute walk away. Overall, this is without a doubt one of the best hotels in Hong Kong and probably in Asia. I highly recommend staying here.

<Author>hhelena
<Content>Excellent hotel, wonderful service, great location We stayed four nights in a Club room in early May. Everything was great about this hotel, from the pickup within moments we arrived at the airport until they dropped us of again four days later (we prebooked the limo service, very efficient email response from the hotel). The location is also brilliant, with old style Hong Kong outside the door and new shiny Hong Kong 10 minutes away on the MTR. Buy an octopus card as soon as you get there, it is the easiest way to travel, it is a type of cash card that you load with money and then use for all your travel needs, MTR, buses etc. You can even use it for shopping, we ended up using it everywhere rather than cash. Public transport is very cheap and superefficient.The hotel itself is spotless, with the most wonderful fragrance everywhere and the staff is lovely. They were always very helpful and friendly with not the slightest hint of snootiness. We had an excecutive Club room which gives you access to the Club lounge on the 36th floor. This is a wonderful calm place to chill out with a drink in the evening, overlooking the hustle and bustle of Hong Kong. The main bar downstairs is very popular and quite noisy so it was nice to chill out with a quiet drink upstairs before going to bed in the evening. The Club lounge is open 24 hours and you have free access to hot and cold drinks, cocktails, some very nice wines, several different kinds of beer, various nibbles, little mini desserts (and very nice too!) etc. This is also where you check in and out if you have booked a Club room. When you are in a Club room breakfast is included, either in the Club lounge or you can take it downstairs in the main breakfast room. The lounge is more quiet of course but the choice is bigger downstairs, with everything from traditional congee and dim sum to the full English, if that is what you like. It was probably the best breakfast buffet we have ever come across. Everything was of excellent quality and the staff very attentive. If you dont fancy eating in the hotel, just walk out the door, the Langham mall is just next door with a large food court, or head out on the streets for some local flavours! There is literally gazillions of options just around the corner.The room itself (on the 35th floor) was of good size, plasma tv and all other mod cons, the airconditioning was easy to control and worked, the bed very comfortable with a mountain of pillows, plus a pillow menu if you fancied even more or different style, including scented pilows. The view over Hong Kong was wonderful, could not have been better, we were overlooking Hong Kong island and Victoria peak. The bathroom was also lovely with a great rainshower and separate bathtub. The evening turndown service also serviced the room, tidying up, checking the towels etc so the room was actually tidied up twice a day! Also left some gorgeous chocolate to look forward to every night....The swimmingpool is on the 42nd floor so needless to say the view is wonderful. It is quite a small roof top area so the sunloungers were often all taken in the afternoon, but it didnt really bother us as we just wanted to cool down with a quick swim before heading out again. Some previous reviewers seems to have issues with the location, however, we felt that it was by far the best location in all of Hong Kong for us. Mongkok is still retaining some old style, where locals still live, and shop. There is a faboulus local food market at the back of the hotel, OK, it is not for the faint hearted as all sorts of living creatures are for sale for the dinnertable, but for us that is what travelling is all about. It is a perfectly safe area, just use your common sense as in all large cities. We wandered around the streets at night, ate at street food stalls and generally had a great time and then went back to our wonderful quiet room for a good nights sleep. When we return to Hong Kong we will definitely be staying here again, as it is one of the best hotels we have ever had the pleasure to stay in.

<Author>benthere
<Content>Weak start, strong finish If not for a poor start, I would consider rating this hotel as excellent. To begin, the hotel has a visitor's desk at the airport where you can get transportation to the hotel at a reasonable rate (good). Regrettably, the clerk put me on a bus to the wrong hotel (bad). Not a big deal. Mistakes happen. They quickly rectified it by having a limo pick me up quickly and transport me to the correct property. I arrived there at 3:30 P.M. and was notified that they had granted some guests a late checkout and that my room wouldn't be ready until 9:00. 5-1/2 HOURS LATER! Why they granted guests such a late checkout is beyond me! I was perturbed, to say the least. The clerk tried to assuage me with a coupon for a free drink at the bar, but this only angered me more. I went for a walk to kill time and returned at 8:30 to find that my room was ready. After midnight, the phone woke me up 3 times. Apparently, someone in another room was calling the wrong number. I was a bit annoyed that the operator wouldn't tell me who it was or that she didn't offer to call that person and ask them to stop the calls. Eventually, I set the phone on DND and that put an end to it. To be honest, I needed a full day to get past a horrid start. But I'll give credit where credit is due. The hotel rebounded strongly! First, the room was very clean and comfortable and it is connected via a walkway to Langham Place shopping center. It is also right next to Mongkok transit station. They have the best fitness center of any hotel I've ever been at in addtion to numerous holistic therapy offerings. It's quite impressive! The staff is extremely courteous and friendly. The hotel has an internet access area with about 8 PC's or laptops that are free for the guests to use. There was always one available when I went there. I ate at one of their restaurants (the name escapes me) and had a very good meal. During one of my stops at their internet access center, I accessed their website and sent some feedback about my disatisfaction with the start to my stay there. I was pleasantly surprised to return to my room that evening and find a message from a manager apologizing for the problems and asking to discuss them with me. I never got a chance to talk to him because of my schedule. However, we corresponded via email and he removed the bus fare charge to the hotel and the limo charge back to the airport from my bill - a generous and appreciated gesture. Finally, I should mention that the concierge desk was extremely helpful and made things very conveneint. I should cite Eddie Ho in particular. He couldn't have been nicer and went beyond my expectations as to assisting me. In summary, I give the hotel the benefit of the doubt and chalk the poor start up to a bad decision on their part, but then they made up for it after that. I would probably stay there again.

<Author>Miss_Pie
<Content>Lovely hotel in bustling Mongkok Enjoyed our stay at this hotel very much. We booked it because of the recommendations on tripadvisor and we were definitely not disappointed. We booked directly with the hotel and included breakfast with this package. I would recommend that you take the breakfast as it is an excellent buffet with a huge choice of food. We also booked the limo from the airport which made our journey from the airport less stressful. The staff at all times were very pleasant and helpful. Although the bedrooms are not the largest that I have stayed in they are very well appointed and have all the amenities that are necessary with lots of lovely toiletries in the bathroom. The room was immaculately maintained and we were never disturbed in the room yet it had always been serviced when we returned to the hotel in the afternoon/evening. The hotel also has a lovely pool on the roof. Apart from the hotel and adjacent mall the surrounding area is not particularly upmarket and if I had known this when I had been booking the hotel I would probably not have gone there but in fact it was not a problem and we never felt threatened at any time. I was happy to walk in the vicinity of the hotel on my own without my husband. Although the hotel is slightly further out from the centre this is not a problem as it is adjacent to the MTR which takes you all over Hong Kong quickly and at a very reasonable price. Again it is clean and very safe. If I were returning to Hong Kong I would certainly stay again at this hotel as you get luxury at a very reasonable price.

<Author>ktmack89
<Content>FANTASTIC! A+ HIGHLY RECOMMEND TO ANYONE! BEST SERVICE! 5 stars overall!!!! The Langham Place in Mongkok has A+++ service! It is a beautiful hotel with various facitilies to suit families and business travellers.The service at this hotel is 5 stars. The staff are always friendly, willing to help, and will give you information where ever you need. Every single person who we encountered were fantastic and provided only the best customer service. As for the rooms they were presented beautifully and the option to choose a scented pillow for your individual needs is great. The room also has internet access in which you can connect to broadband services and there is also basic internet browsing on the tv. The other technology is the CISCO phones which allow you to get information about Hong Kong, foreign currency rates and you able to view maps on the screen. The ipod/mp3 dock was also very useful in this day in age when everyone has one. The higher levels in which were staying were great you could see a great view! Overall very impressed with the rooms! This trip was certainly made better by the club L room - this level gives you free access to the internet, various books to read, a FANTASTIC view, and food and drinks always on hand. The best thing about this is that it is open 24hrs and there is always people on hand to help you - either for directions or different enquires. However the other facilities are great with an extensive gym, sauna,pool, spa, sitting rooms and dining areas.The location is great! It is in central Mongkok and there are various shops just across the street. I appreciated the accessibility to everything - for those tourists there were the ladies markets and various other attractions. The MTR is right nearby and therefore makes it easy to get to around Hong Kong. So overall with the helpful people, the lovely rooms, the location of the place and the great facilities it combines to make it a pleasurable hotel to stay. Would defintely stay there again! 5 stars!

<Author>wilytraveller
<Content>Great stay but one issue Booked directly with the Hotel and stayed over New Year. Emailed them requesting a car service from the Airport and received a prompt reply. Service was very efficient at the hotel desk in the airport to the car.The Hotel is right next to the Mongkok MTR subway and transport links are truly excellent both to the airport and Hong Kong island. Mongkok is busy, with a very high people density.I'd booked a suite on their club floor and hence checked-in at the Club Lounge on 36th which was pleasant change from the normal hotel hassle. The club itself has great views and the service from the butlers is excellent.The room itself is a little bit on the small size, but not a big issue. Everything was of very high quality, including the plasma tv! The restaurant on the ground floor for breakfast was excellent as was the gym/swimming pool facilities.The only issue we encountered was that my wife suffered from food poisoning - presumably at the hands of hotel food given we'd only eaten in the hotel for the previous 24hrs.The hotel staff responded extremely well, getting an english speaking doctor (actually he had trained as a doctor in Birmingham, UK!) and paying for him. However, a day and half was knocked out of our holiday because of this.I've previously stayed at the JW Marriot at Admiralty, Hong Kong island which was more convenient as a base for access to both Kowloon and Central. However, Langham Place is a very good hotel (and more reasonably priced that the top hotels on the island) so as long as your happy to be put out by 10min or so travel, I'd highly recommend staying here.

<Author>Traveller885
<Content>Superb Hotel As most reviewers here have noted, this is an absolute gem of a hotel with amenities and facilities that are generally in the almost 5 star hotel class at much less than 5 star prices. The only significant drawback is the smallish room sizes, which also means that there isn't much furniture to sit on in a Club L Room other than the bed. (There is one desk chair and one none-too-comfortable sitting chair, so for two people, watching TV has to be done from bed.) However, the bed is ultra-comfortable and the choice of pillows (which you can select in advance of arrival from a pillow menu) is excellent, easily matching the beds, pillows and linens of the Peninsula or any Four Seasons.Other than the small room sizes, it's a top-notch place, with a friendly and generally helpful staff, a superb club lounge (with free internet access and beverage service 24/7, and a fine array of snacks put out at various times of day), a heated outdoor pool that is one of the better ones in town, and the advantage, on rainy days, of being connected to a sizable shopping mall. The Club L lounge furnishings are lavish and spacious, and on non-cloudy days, the view from the lounge is special.Breakfast in the lobby level restaurant is comprehensive, with various pastries and breads, an array of cold cuts, both Japanese foods and a small selection of dim sum, a variety of cereals, made to order omelets, bacon, sausages, pancakes, yogurts, and a wonderful choice of fresh fruits and fresh fruit juices, including not just your standards (e.g., organge juice, grapefruit juice, apple juice, etc.), but watermelon juice and others. Most people who indulge a bit at breakfast won't find themselves wanting to have lunch at all.The rooms are cleaned several times a day by a fastidious, truly remarkable staff. If you use their shower cap, they will replace it with a new one. They make sure that the bathroom is spotless, as well.I recommend this place enthusiastically.

<Author>DLPA
<Content>I stay here EVERYTIME I'm in HK. I totally love this hotel! The rooms are sizeable and clean, the bathrooms are fantastic, the bed is SO comfortable. The location is in the now revamped 'cool' area of town Mongkok where there's tonnes of food to eat, and a trendy young shopping mall with cinema connected straight to the hotel. Stay here if you don't mind commuting to HK island!

<Author>jakester20
<Content>Langham Place 鈥?Many Great Amenities  My wife, my 16-year-old daughter and I just completed a six-day/six night vacation at the Langham Place during April 2008. It was very, very enjoyable for many reasons and I鈥檒l break down the hotel and our experience based on Location, Rooms, Amenities, Staff and Restaurants for everybody to review and make their own choices. Each category will be rated on scale of 1-5, with 1 being horrible and 5 Outstanding We all would definitely stay there again, and for those who are making their first trip to Hong Kong we both loved the city and entire six days.Location 鈥?Overall Rating 4The location from out point of view could be broken down based on access to transportation, neighborhood, and Kowloon or Hong Kong side of city. Transportation and LinkagesThe spot is good; not great. Hong Kong is a walking city and has a terrific public transportation system. The Mong Kong location with the MTR adjacent to the hotel was great. However, there are better locations with comparable locations either on Hong Kong Island at Central or Admiralty stop or on Kowloon side at YTR stop. Very nice and easy to get anywhere and would not hesitate to stay again. 4.5 subsection ratingNeighborhoodThe Mong Kong neighborhood has some very nice features and OK features. First, the hotel is adjacent to Langham Place, a vertical in fill mall. It鈥檚 not a super deluxe mall, but more mid 鈥?level with many nice stores, but not many luxury brands. I would suggest that the neighborhood reminds me of Times Square in New York. Every conceivable retailer imaginable available and people all over the place. For those who love to shop at the Hong Kong markets a few blocks from the hotel is the Ladies Market. Yes, my wife and daughter made it there twice and loved it. Finally, there鈥檚 not many restaurant or other options outside the hotel so for those who don鈥檛 want to leave the neighborhood this might not be the place for them. 3.5 subsection rating.Kowoon or Hong Kong IslandThis is a toss up for anybody. However, after my week in HK, I would suggest that Honk Kong Island would be preferable to Kowloon Island. There鈥檚 definitely more of everything. We found ourselves going to Hong Kong Island almost daily. Most of the ferries to the outer islands leave from Hong Kong Island. Frankly, but for the laser light show, which must be seen from Kowloon Island and the view of Hong Kong Island is your staying at the Intercontinental or other comparable hotel with drop dead fabulous view of Hong Kong island I can鈥檛 see why would want to stay here. 4 subsection rating.Rooms Rating 5It鈥檚 hard to say much bad about the rooms. We had a 600 sf suite for around $375/night. I felt that was a very nice deal. We were located on the club level, what they call Level L. it was very nice and the room was very nice. Nice linens, two flat screen TV鈥檚, nice washroom, great view, etc. Could not of been better. Staff Rating 5This is easy. They could not of tried harder to please; top to bottom. From the moment we checked into the hotel after flying 15 hours non-stop from Chicago to when we checked out, each and every staff member was extremely accomadating. This did not just stop in the concierge lounge, but included everybody at the hotel from maintenance, housekeeping, attendants in the gym, etc. Amenities Rating 5Both in the hotel and surrounding the hotel they were terrific. To start with the hotel is connected to the Langham Place mall. Not super luxury, but very nice with lots of fast food restaurants and a Starbucks right out the door from the hotel lobby on the 4th floor. Additionally, the MTR was right next to the Langham Place. You could access either from the interior of the mall or a short walk outside. Terrific.However, hotel amenities nothing to sneeze at. Hotel spa was wonderful. We had two separate treatments and the therapists were wonderful. Wished they were closer to me 100% of the time. The exercise room/gym was fully equipped. Though we did not use the pool, we viewed it and it鈥檚 a wow experience. Hard to beat. Restaurants Rating 5We solely went to The Place, which was their continental restaurant and Ming Court, which was where we enjoyed Dim Sung. Both were wonderful. We had breakfast every day at The Place. Was great. The hotel buffet breakfast was terrific and included a number of items that were traditional, English, Asian and a combination. Terrific. Ming Court was great. Frankly, it seemed to be frequented more by locals than guests at the hotel I consider this a good thing.SummaryOk. So I loved the hotel and loved Hong Kong. Yes, I did. With the exception of the slightly offbeat location, this was a five in every other category. That being said, it鈥檚 totally impossible going wrong at the Langham Place and I would highly recommend for either a vacation of business trip to Hong Kong
